Lawyer Zhu Sifu Requests Severe Punishment for Ke Yinghao

If it is proven that he has become a Japanese citizen

Then he should be sent to the Japanese Consulate for punishment

Lawyer Zhu Sifu, representing Liu Yide's rental property, has accused Fujian native Ke Yinghao of owing more than 1,000 yuan in rent for No. 5, Pingle Lane, Xizang Road. On the 10th of this month, when Judge Luo Chongtai of the First Special District Court heard the case in Civil Court No. 7, Ke claimed to be a Japanese citizen and not under jurisdiction. Lawyer Zhu immediately requested the court to order Ke to produce his certificate of renunciation of Chinese nationality, according to the Nationality Law. This angered Ke, who wanted to assault Lawyer Zhu. Court officers stopped him, preventing an unfortunate incident. Details were reported in this newspaper on the 11th. Lawyer Zhu believes that this kind of incident is not only an insult to an individual but also a contempt of court. If he is not severely punished, how can national law be upheld? Therefore, he submitted a report to the Lawyers Association, requesting that it be forwarded to the First Special District Court, requesting that Ke be severely punished. The report was sent to the Lawyers Association yesterday. The original text is recorded below: Regarding the report, Liu Yide, a representative of a member, filed a lawsuit in the Civil Court of the First Special District Court against Ke Yinghao, a Fujian native residing at No. 5, Pingle Lane, Xizang Road, for owing more than 1,000 yuan in rent. When Judge Luo Chongtai of the First Special District Court summoned him to Civil Court No. 7 on the 10th of this month, the member representative, the plaintiff, appeared in court, and Ke Yinghao also appeared in court. He stated that he was originally from Shanghang County, Fujian Province, and that in the 8th year of the Republic (1919), a Mr. Ji from the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai applied to the Ministry of Interior of our country for renunciation of his Chinese nationality. In the 9th year of the Republic (1920), he officially became a Japanese citizen. Therefore, he is not under the jurisdiction of our national court, and he submitted a Japanese citizenship certificate as proof. At that time, the member immediately based on Article 11 of the Nationality Law, which states that the renunciation of nationality by the people must have a certificate of renunciation of nationality from the Ministry of Interior of our country to be valid. Ke Yinghao only submitted a certificate of naturalization but not a certificate of renunciation, so he cannot be recognized as a Japanese citizen according to law. Unexpectedly, at this time, Ke stepped down from the defendant's box and strode back and forth in front of the judge's seat. Although the judge stopped him, it was to no avail, and he even transferred his anger to the member, raising his fist to strike the member. Fortunately, he was stopped by court officials, avoiding assault. However, Ke Yinghao spoke in the Min dialect and insulted and cursed the member, saying that he had to beat him. At that time, he was menacing. Judge Luo then announced that the case would be adjourned to investigate his nationality with the Ministry of Interior and adjourned the court. Ke was still unwilling and waited outside the court, wanting to get the member. After being informed, the member stated this situation to the court at that time. To avoid his attack, he had to temporarily avoid him in the court. After a long time, Ke left the court. This is the situation at that time. The lawyer only knows to represent the party in litigation according to law. If the defendant has any defense, he can make a legitimate statement to the court based on legal principles. He cannot transfer his anger to the agent lawyer. Now, Ke Yinghao relies on being a Japanese citizen and dares to act arbitrarily in the dignified court, even attempting to beat the member in court. Regardless of nationality, the order of the court should be strictly observed. If there is a violation, the judge can place him in custody and send him to the consulate for investigation. Moreover, it is difficult to prove whether Ke Yinghao has indeed become a Japanese citizen before the Ministry of Interior replies. Now he is so violent. If he is formally a Japanese citizen, I don't know how violent he will be. Ke's behavior is not only an insult to the member but also damages the prestige of our country's courts. Insulting the member is a small matter, and disrespecting the dignity of the national court is a big matter. There are few houses and many people, which is extremely detrimental to health and public morals. More greedy people built five-story shacks on the drying platform with only air circulation. If you are not careful, a fire will easily spread. Once there is a fire, nothing will be left. Reasons for the Congestion of Postal Parcels

Customs Inspection Takes Time

The other day, the newspaper reported that the people of the city felt that the post office and postal parcels were very congested, and it took a lot of time to send the parcels out, which caused complaints. They planned to ask the post office to find a way to improve it. The reporter from the Central News Agency inquired about the post office. According to the person in charge, the postal authorities have ordered the Shanghai Postal Administration to find a way to improve it as soon as possible to facilitate it. However, the reason for the congestion is that the customs has exempted the parcels sent and received by the post office from transshipment tax, so the number of pieces has increased sharply. However, although the transshipment tax is exempted, the customs inspection procedures are still the same, and they must be inspected one by one, resulting in backlog congestion. The people who send the parcels have to wait for a long time and misunderstandings occur.

Assassination in a Tram

Chief Detective Zhou Honglin Shot

The Murderer Fired a Gun Separated by the Doors of the First and Third Classes

Zhou Honglin, a native of Yancheng, 34 years old, lived in Jinyuanli, Datong Road, Avenue Edward VII, Public Concession. He served as a detective in the Criminal Investigation Department of the Fuzhou Road Police Station for several years. He was very serious in his work, so he was trusted by his superiors. Zhou never prepared a car to go home after work. He must take the Public Concession's Route 16 or Route 19 trolleybus. Yesterday afternoon at 12:00 p.m., Zhou took Route 16 trolleybus No. 300 to return home for lunch after finishing his official business. On the way, he happened to meet Detective Xu Zhenting of the Xinzha Police Station and Chinese policeman Zhang Shaobo of the Jiaxing Road Police Station, who also took the same bus to return home. Since they knew each other, they greeted each other briefly and chatted side by side. When the bus arrived at the Enterprise Company station at No. 517, Avenue Edward VII, more than a dozen passengers got off the bus, and at the same time two or three passengers got on the bus, so it was very crowded. When the bus got off, there were only one or two passengers left. When the conductor was about to ring the bell to start the bus and close the door, two male passengers in the third-class seat, one wearing a yellow gown and the other wearing an overcoat, suddenly got off the bus in a hurry. The conductor thought that they had missed the station, so he reopened the door for them. Unexpectedly, in a short time, the man wearing the overcoat took out a box gun and fired two shots at Zhou Honglin from across the glass door between the first and third classes. The glass was pierced with two holes, and the bullets hit Zhou's head and waist. Immediately, blood flowed like a waterfall, and he fell in the car. The murderer, seeing that the goal had been achieved, jumped off the trolleybus and fled. At that time, Xu Zhenting and Zhang Shaobo witnessed this situation, so they ordered the bus to stop immediately and drew their guns to chase down. Seeing that the murderers had turned into Jinjiazhai and fled, they hurried up, but the alley was intricate and they escaped. Xu and others rushed to the Xinzha Police Station to report. They immediately called an ambulance to rush Zhou to the Public Works Bureau Hospital for treatment. Because the injuries were in key areas, the situation was very critical. They also unloaded the glass that had been shot through and brought it back to the police station for research, and asked the passengers who witnessed it in detail about the appearance of the murderer and sent out a strict search.

Cessation of Trial Proceedings; Release of Lu Xihou and Others on Bail

The Judge Views Lu's Progress in Clearing Debts

As a Reference for Adjudicating the Accusation Against Him

Following the collapse of the Banque Industrielle de Chine, the Legal Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council considered the bank's Chairman, Lu Xihou, the Deputy Manager, Lu Mengxiang, and the Manager of the Xinhua Trading Company, Sun Xiren, to be jointly involved in fraud. It therefore brought a lawsuit in the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, alleging incomplete records in the bank's account books. Important officers of the bank, Wan Weijian and Zhou Shaopeng, etc., were also prosecuted under company law in the same case. The First Special District Court has conducted several hearings. These matters have been detailed in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, opened the criminal court to continue the hearing. Tao Youxin, the British accountant engaged by the police to investigate the accounts, also appeared in court. Judge Qian questioned Tao about the doubts in his report and ordered him to swear an oath of responsibility, stating that the facts in the report were true. He also inquired of Lu Xihou about the Wang Guozhi mortgage incident. Immediately afterward, he proceeded to hear the portions of the case against the defendants accused of violating company regulations. Only the defendant Zhou Shaopeng appeared in court; the others were absent. The police lawyer, Ru Bao Yi, stated the reasons for the prosecution, announcing that the charges against the absent defendants would be withdrawn, and requesting that those present be judged according to the law. Lu Xihou's lawyers, Wu Lin Kun and Fan Gang, briefly stated the facts. Judge Qian then instructed Lu Xihou that the presiding judge could independently judge whether he was guilty or innocent according to the law. However, if found guilty, he would definitely not settle his debts, and if found innocent, he would be even less willing to do so. Therefore, in order to protect the interests of the creditors, the trial was suspended to observe his progress in clearing his debts, as a reference for the judgment. The court ruled that the trial proceedings regarding Lu Xihou, Sun Xiren, and Lu Mengxiang be suspended. Lu Xihou was allowed to be released from custody upon payment of 20,000 yuan in cash and 30,000 yuan in surety bonds. However, if the judge deemed it necessary to detain him during the liquidation process, he could still be detained. The court also issued judgments on the parts of the case concerning the defendants accused under company law. Zhou Shaopeng and Wan Weijian were both found not guilty. The cases against Chen Jikan, Xiang Xiang, Wu Lihua, Feng Weiqin, Lu Ruizheng, Wang Qi, Lu Xifan, and Wang Jixuan were not accepted.

Extortion Under False Pretense of Court's Name is Urgent

Zhao Yongliang and He Shouming Are Extremely Despicable

Police Arrest and Prosecute After Disturbance in Front of the Court

Zhou Fugen, a local resident residing at No. 3 Ruyi Lane, Lan Weiai Road, in the French Concession, was found to have supplied handguns and shared the spoils in a robbery case. Detectives Wang Rusong and Liu Jinrong of the French police learned of this. First, the robbers were apprehended and based on their confessions, Zhou and his wife, Wang (26 years old this year), were arrested by the police on October 30th of last year and sent to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. On November 9th, the police formally filed a public prosecution. During the trial, it was found that there was no suspicion of criminal activity on the part of Zhou and Wang, and they were released in court without prosecution. Zhou Fugen was prosecuted for the crime of illegally possessing military weapons, and the trial concluded on November 26th with a fine of 300 yuan. However, after Zhou Wang was released, she went around seeking people to help her find ways to reduce her husband's sentence. At that time, Zhao Yongliang, a Nanjing native, 28 years old this year, residing at No. 1 Liangyi Lane, Dafang Lane, in the Chinese district, and He Shouming (also known as Hu Bin, 35 years old this year, from Nanjing, residing at No. 5 Songshou Lane, Xin Zha Road, who previously worked as a dispatcher in the Second Special District Court Detention Center and was dismissed for cause, and has been idle lately), were two people who usually lingered in front of the Second Special District Court, soliciting bail, soliciting lawsuits, and swindling. Zhao and He were acquainted with Liu Kezhong, Zhou Wang's sub-landlord. Through Liu's introduction, they met Zhou Wang. Zhao and He then bragged that they knew various judges in the court and could help with lobbying, and could guarantee a reduced sentence, but required a fee of 500 yuan. Zhou Wang vaguely agreed. After the court's judgment, Zhou Fugen was fined, believing that they had voluntarily done so, and demanded a reward of 500 yuan from Zhou Wang. Because of her difficult circumstances and the fact that her husband was imprisoned, she could not afford it and asked for a delay. Zhao and He were impatient, and on November 29th, they urged Zhou Wang to issue a note, and because she was a woman and could not make decisions, they asked her to invite a man to the scene. Zhou had no choice but to invite her father, Zhou Guanyun (56 years old, who runs a rattan chair shop in Tilanqiao) to the scene, and after Wang's repeated requests, the amount was reduced by 100 yuan, and Zhou Guanyun issued a promissory note for 400 yuan, accruing interest according to the code, and to be delivered in ten days. When the time came, Zhao and He again urged Zhou Wang to pay, and she promised to wait until her husband was released to raise the money. Unexpectedly, Zhao and others forced Zhou Wang to sell her furniture to pay off the debt, limiting the time to do so and then dispersed. On the 14th of this month, at noon, Zhou Wang brought clothes and food to the Second Special District Court Detention Center to visit her husband. She met Zhao and He in front of the court, and they again urged her to pay, surrounding her and forcing her to sell her furniture to pay immediately. At this point, Zhou Wang could not delay any longer and started an argument. After the argument, she reported to the French police, accusing Zhao and He of intimidation and extortion. The police chief then sent detectives Wang Rusong, Zhang Daorong, and Wang Dongwan to the front of the Second Special District Court to arrest Zhao and He. Evidence of fraud was found on them: a list of names of judges and prosecutors from the Second Special District Court, the Primary and Local Courts, and the Third Branch Court, as well as clerks, a business card of the police lawyer, a promissory note issued by Zhou Guanyun, and many miscellaneous notes. After questioning by the police chief, they were ordered to be detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer, Yuan Jiahuang, stated the case and requested a postponement in order to conduct a detailed investigation and file a lawsuit for trial, and presented the seized evidence. Zhou Wang and Zhou Guanyun then testified about the previous situation. After the judge examined the presented evidence and various notes, he was greatly angered by the fact that the two defendants falsely used the names of court judges and prosecutors to swindle money. After separate interrogations, both defendants made evasive remarks, denying that they had falsely used names to deceive, claiming that the plaintiff had asked people to find bail for her husband, and that the promissory note was a guarantee for the bail, not extortion. After reviewing the confessions in court, the court ordered a postponement of the hearing to the 26th of this month, and the defendants were returned to custody.

Gao Weixiang, a photography expert who studied in Germany and was previously known in the photography community for creating the exposure meter timer, observed that the failure of general photography is attributed to the error in exposure time. Not only do beginners in photography have no grasp of the determination of exposure time, but even those with more experience in photography also find it difficult in particularly difficult situations and in the exchange of new experiences, resulting in wasted money and missed opportunities, which is very regrettable. According to expert investigation, at least 70% of the films have exposure errors. Although there are already various exposure meters to help, it is impossible to find one that is easy to use and accurately calculates. Therefore, he specially researched and developed the only perfect "Zheqin-style exposure meter" based on many years of research on exposure problems. No matter where or when, indoors or outdoors, just move it lightly to get the correct exposure time for taking photos and videos, eliminating the need for thinking or measuring. The results are completely the same as the most accurate photoelectric method, but it is easy to use and low in price, which is not its reach. Various still cameras and movie cameras can be applied. With various charts and explanations, it is very practical. He has already applied for patent rights in various countries. Since its release, it has been printed in various languages ​​and sold to hundreds of thousands at home and abroad. The complexity of China's economic organization and the chaos of its current situation make it impossible for the general public to understand. There are few good books on the market that can provide a concise analysis and a simple introduction. The Shen Bao Monthly of the Shen Bao Newspaper, in view of this, specially invited domestic economists to compile the book "Talks on the Current Situation of China's Economy" and listed it as one of the company's series of books. The current situation of China's economy is divided into eight lectures, namely (1) Overview, (2) Finance, (3) Domestic and Foreign Trade, (4) Agriculture, (5) Industry, (6) Transportation, (7) Economic Power of the Great Powers in China, and (8) Way Out. Each lecture uses simple language to make a systematic description. Those who have no economic knowledge at ordinary times can get a clear concept of the entire current situation of China's economy after reading it once. The last lecture, "The Way Out of China's National Economy," is especially wonderful and worthy of Chinese people to ponder. The book was published on the 15th of this month and is priced at six jiao. It is also heard that those who subscribe to the Shen Bao Monthly for the whole year before the end of February will receive a copy as a gift. A coupon for the book is attached to the New Year's issue of the Shen Bao Monthly.

A Resplendent and Glamorous Occasion

Shanghai Banks and Others Continue to Provide Fertilizer Loans of 500,000 Yuan to Shaanxi Province

One Yuan Per Mu, 500,000 Mu Scheduled

And Promote Farmers' Cooperatives in the Province

Shanghai, Jin Cheng, Jiao Tong, Zhejiang Industrial and other Five Banks, organized a cotton industry production and sales cooperative banking group, and after providing cotton industry loans in Shaanxi, now continue to provide fertilizer loans of 500,000 yuan. The details are as follows:

Cotton Loans Take Effect

In addition to organizing a banking group, the above-mentioned five banks signed a contract with the Shaanxi Cotton Industry Improvement Institute under the Cotton Industry Control Committee to provide cotton industry loans. At the same time, the Shanghai Bank independently provided cotton industry loans. Since the implementation, it has been quite effective. The first batch of more than 500 bales of cotton produced by the Farmers' Cooperatives has arrived in Shanghai. Now the above-mentioned five banks have decided to promote cotton land, and this year the scheduled cotton land has been expanded from more than 200,000 mu to 500,000 mu to promote it.

Continue to Lend Fertilizer

Now that the cotton has been harvested and it is time for winter fertilization, the Shanghai Bank has begun to provide Shaanxi cotton industry fertilizer loans. In addition to taking on 200,000 yuan itself, it will jointly undertake 300,000 yuan with various banking group banks, totaling 500,000 yuan. It is stipulated that the fertilizer for each mu of cotton land will be loaned at one yuan. This year, cotton land in Shaanxi Province has been promoted to 500,000 mu, so 500,000 yuan is required. The farmers in the province are also very trusting of the above-mentioned five banks.

Special Article

Peng Xiangying's Speech on the Relationship Between Citizens and Air Defense (Continued)

Therefore, since we know the terror of fires caused by incendiary bombs and the difficulty of firefighting during air raids, we should organize fire self-defense teams or fire prevention squads in peacetime and enthusiastically engage in training, and strive to purchase firefighting equipment to supplement the shortcomings of the fire brigade in wartime.

Now, let us take the benefits of air defense equipment and organization already in place in Japan, for peacetime, when dealing with the occurrence of disasters, as an example to see that air defense equipment can not only protect our lives and property in wartime but also prevent the spread of our peacetime disasters. Because Japan feels that the air forces of various countries are developed and the range of flight has expanded, it is afraid that its islands of Fusang will be easily attacked by air. From the perspective of its national defense and strategy, it is actively engaged in air defense equipment. In recent years, in its important cities across the country, it has spared no expense to make efforts in various air defense facilities and carry out large-scale air defense exercises. Since it carried out its first air defense exercise in Osaka in Showa 3 (i.e., our Republic of China 17), it followed up with the Nagoya air defense exercise in Showa 4, the Kyushu air defense exercise in Showa 6, and the Tokyo air defense exercise in Showa 8. Last August, it also carried out a large-scale air defense exercise in Osaka. In the meantime, there are still small-scale air defense exercises in various cities, even in its colonies such as Gyeongseong in Korea and Taiwan, which also held air defense exercises. It can be seen that Japan's efforts in air defense are no less than those of other countries in the world. Japan, which has never been attacked by enemy aircraft, is still so concerned about air defense facilities. Shouldn't we, this naked city with unhealed wounds, quickly seek protective facilities? Last July, I wanted to know about the air defense situation in Japan, so I went to Japan to visit the Osaka air defense exercise. Only then did I know that their exercise was prepared for a year and cost hundreds of thousands of dollars. When the exercise took place, the participating troops had the mobilization of four divisions, and the participating people also had more than ten million. In addition to the 1st and 3rd flight regiments, the 7th bombing regiment, and the Akeno Flight School and naval aircraft, newspaper aircraft, transportation company aircraft, etc., about 70 aircraft participated in the exercise. There were also 48 anti-aircraft guns from the 1st anti-aircraft artillery regiment and various field artillery regiments, 28 searchlights and listening devices, and more than 200 anti-aircraft machine guns and anti-aircraft machine guns deployed in the Kyoto, Osaka, and Kobe areas to serve as military air defense exercises. There were also six barrage balloons from the Chiba Air Defense Balloon Team raised in the air to prevent enemy aircraft. In addition, the agencies participating in the exercise included the Osaka Railway Bureau, the Nagoya Railway Bureau, the Osaka Communications Bureau, the Nagoya Communications Bureau, the Osaka Customs, the Kobe Customs, and the various agencies and schools under the jurisdiction of the central government, the Ministry of Communications, and the Ministry of Railways in various prefectures, cities, districts, townships, and villages. Almost everyone in the exercise area participated. The most noteworthy thing for us is the protection corps, which bears the heavy responsibility of civil air defense. The protection corps is the only agency for citizens to prevent air raids. It is a group that serves to reduce or avoid damage when enemy aircraft drop bombs, incendiary bombs, and gas bombs. The group is composed of members of the veterans' association, members of the youth corps, students of the youth training institute (such as our country's student army, boy scouts, etc.), firefighters, members of neighborhood self-government associations, medical and health groups, women's groups, etc. The group headquarters is located in the Osaka Municipal Government. According to the 15 districts in the city, each district organizes a district protection corps. Under the district, a protection branch is set up according to each protection area. Under the branch, there are various classes to directly undertake protection duties. The organizational situation of the protection corps is as follows:

Osaka City Protection Corps | District Protection Corps | Protection Branch | ((1) Security Class (2) Alarm Class) (3) Fire Prevention Class (4) Traffic Control Class (5) Shelter Management Class (6) Evacuee Guidance Class (7) Work Class (8) Poison Gas Prevention Class (9) Rescue Class (10) Supply Class (11) Propaganda Class (12) Liaison Class

During this exercise, the Osaka City Protection Corps had a total of 280 branches, totaling 171,500 members. In addition, there were 902 factory protection corps branches, totaling 174,725 people, all organized by male and female workers and staff from various factories in Osaka to be responsible for the protection of factories during air raids. The above totaled nearly 350,000 people, all of whom had received air defense training in peacetime and possessed air defense knowledge and skills, and the organization was very strict. Even if it is not an air defense exercise period, it can be convened at any time to deal with various disasters. For example, last September, when Osaka suffered a major disaster of hurricanes and floods, Osaka achieved a lot of results in the emergency rescue at the time and the post-disaster reconstruction due to the efforts of the protection corps. It is conceivable that if it is such a natural disaster that cannot be prevented, it will be able to exert its ability to achieve the purpose of passive air defense in the face of man-made air raids.

In short, in Osaka City, Japan, there are 300,000 protection corps members organized by citizens. The air defense organization and facilities of other important cities and towns can also be inferred. Here, we not only know that the Japanese people's attention to and enthusiasm for air defense are no less than those of the British and French people, but we also know that air defense equipment and organization are indeed very effective in preventing disasters in peacetime. Now, let us take the Great Kanto Earthquake in Japan as an example to make us know that without air defense equipment and organization, it is impossible to prevent disasters from occurring in peacetime. During the Great Kanto Earthquake, there were 135 fires in Tokyo at the same time. The flames covered the sky, and the prosperous city turned into hell. However, 43 of the fires were extinguished by the citizens at the beginning of the fire. At this time, many houses collapsed in Tokyo, and the streets were blocked. If the citizens did not automatically extinguish these 43 fires and waited for the fire brigade to arrive, the entire Tokyo would be reduced to ashes. However, considering that the citizens of Tokyo at that time did not have a fire organization with the concept of air raids, if it were today, the damage would be reduced even more. Moreover, air raids have air defense warnings that can be transmitted, and the danger can be foreseen in advance, and citizens can have sufficient preparation time. Even if the incendiary bombs dropped are fierce, they cannot all hit the target. If they can be rescued with effort at the time, the damage from the fire can be reduced. Then, under this clear proof, we should quickly engage in air defense facilities and not wait until disaster strikes, digging a well when thirsty, which is too late. (To be continued)

Educational News

Beiping Middle and Primary Schools Implement Strict Examination and Investigation System

Public and Private Middle and Primary Schools Hold Surprise Examinations

The Schools, Classes, and Subjects to Be Tested Are Not Announced in Advance

Subsidies for Private Schools Are Suspended from This Month Onward (Special dispatch from Beiping) There are more than 200 middle and primary schools in Beiping. Some municipal middle schools inevitably have poor performance, and some private middle schools are operated for profit, just like the money-grabbing schools in Shanghai. The quality of primary schools is also uneven. In order to investigate the usual academic performance of students in middle and primary schools, the Social Affairs Bureau has formulated interim measures for surprise examinations in accordance with the "Measures for Investigating the Academic Performance of Middle and Primary Schools" issued by the Ministry of Education and has submitted them to the Ministry of Education for record. At the same time, the Social Affairs Bureau has found that the "Regulations for Subsidizing Private Schools" has been in effect for a long time and is mostly out of touch with reality, and the amount of subsidies allocated is also uneven. Now, in addition to increasing the monthly subsidy by 1,500 yuan starting this year, it has also formulated new subsidy measures and organizational regulations for the "Private School Subsidy Fund Review Committee," and all original subsidies for private schools will be suspended from this month onward. The period from March to May of this year is set as the application period for private schools. All subsidy funds saved from this month to June, estimated at 1,300 yuan per month, will be accumulated until the end of this year and used as a one-time subsidy for schools with particularly excellent performance. The "Measures for Investigating Usual Academic Performance of Middle and Primary Schools," "Measures for Subsidizing Private School Funds," and "Organizational Regulations for the Private School Subsidy Fund Review Committee" are listed as follows:

Investigation Measures

(Article 1) In order to improve the teaching methods of various subjects in middle and primary schools and enhance teaching effectiveness, this Bureau will conduct surprise examinations in accordance with the Ministry's order on measures for investigating students' academic performance. (Article 2) This examination will be organized and handled by a committee organized by the Bureau, consisting of five to nine members, who will be appointed from the following personnel, with the Director of the Bureau as the chairman of the committee: (1) Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, (2) Section Chief of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau and Director of the Middle and Primary School Division, (3) Three or five Supervisors of the Social Affairs Bureau. (Article 3) This examination will be held once a year for middle schools and once a semester for primary schools. The schools, classes, and subjects to be tested will not be announced in advance. (Article 4) The questions for this examination will be formulated by the committee and finalized by the chairman of the committee, and then implemented by the Social Affairs Bureau. (Article 5) The scores for this examination will be calculated using the percentage system, with 60 points as the passing standard. (Article 6) After the examination is completed, the scores will be reviewed and determined by the committee and announced by the Social Affairs Bureau. (Article 7) After the examination is completed, the committee will formulate a plan for improving teaching methods and enhancing effectiveness, which will be reported by the Social Affairs Bureau to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for record and will be followed accordingly. (Article 8) Any matters not covered in these measures may be amended at any time. (Article 9) These measures will be promulgated and implemented from the date of approval by the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government.

Subsidy Measures

(Article 1) The Beiping Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has formulated the "Interim Regulations on Subsidizing Private School Funds" in order to promote the development of private schools. (Article 2) Any private school that meets the following conditions may apply for a subsidy: (A) It has been approved for establishment and has been operating continuously for more than three years with proven results. (B) The school organization, class system, number of students in each class, and curriculum for each subject all comply with the regulations issued by the Ministry and Bureau. (C) The equipment meets the standards set by the regulations. (D) The school's regular expenses are sufficient to maintain its existence. (E) The qualifications of teachers and staff have been approved by the Bureau. (Article 3) All schools applying for a subsidy must submit their applications between March and May of each year, with May 31 as the deadline. (Article 4) After the deadline for subsidy applications, the Bureau will organize a review committee to review and discuss them and report the subsidy amounts decided upon and other matters to the Municipal Government for approval and implementation. (Article 5) After receiving the subsidy, each school should use it as much as possible to enrich its equipment and should report the details of its expenditures for record. (Article 6) The subsidy period is one academic year. After the period expires, the school may continue to apply for a subsidy. (Article 7) If, during the subsidy period, an inspection reveals that the school has violated any of the provisions of Article 2 and Article 5, the subsidy may be suspended. (Article 8) Any matters not covered in these regulations may be amended at any time. (Article 9) These regulations will be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

Organizational Regulations

(Article 1) These regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 4 of the "Interim Regulations on Subsidizing Private School Funds" of the Beiping Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. (Article 2) This committee will have nine members, organized by the following personnel, with the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau as the chairman of the committee: (1) Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, (2) Director of the Education Division of the Municipal Government, (3) Section Chiefs of the First and Third Sections of the Social Affairs Bureau, (4) Three Supervisors of the Social Affairs Bureau, (5) Director of the Middle School Division of the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau. (Article 3) The powers of this committee are as follows: (1) Review applications for subsidies from private schools. (2) Review the standards and amounts of subsidies for private schools. (3) In order to understand the actual operating conditions of each school, in addition to referring to the inspection reports of supervisors, it may conduct on-site investigations if necessary. (Article 4) This committee will hold meetings in the first half of June each year, limited to two weeks. (Article 5) Matters decided by this committee will be reported by the Social Affairs Bureau to the Municipal Government for approval and implementation. (Article 6) In addition to regular meetings, the chairman of the committee may convene special meetings. (Article 7) Any matters not covered in these regulations may be amended at any time. (Article 8) These regulations will be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

Ministry of Education Plans to Produce Tools for Popularizing Compulsory Education and Mass Education

Plans to Invite Experts to Develop Simplified Character Chart

And Cast Copper Molds with Phonetic Annotations for Chinese Characters

The Ministry of Education believes that in order to popularize compulsory education and mass education in various provinces and cities, it is necessary to have simple methods and tools to achieve twice the result with half the effort. It has been noted that during the Song and Ming dynasties, many idle people advocated simplified character charts (such as "Liu" written simply as Liu, "Zhang" written simply as Zhang, etc.), which were popular for a while and passed down through the ages, and may be adopted as tools for promoting compulsory education (because simple "Liu" is easier to recognize and write than complex "Liu," and the same for "Zhang," making it easier for elementary school students and the masses to learn). Also, because Chinese characters are numerous and complex, it is planned to produce copper molds with phonetic annotations for Chinese characters (adding phonetic alphabet annotations next to Chinese characters, so that knowing the phonetic symbols can also be used to spell out and recognize difficult Chinese characters) to assist in popularizing compulsory education and mass education. The Ministry of Education therefore plans to realize this and has already sent letters to Li Shaoxi and Wang Yian, members of the National Language Unification Preparatory Committee, asking them to draft a plan for completing the simplified character chart and casting copper molds with phonetic annotations for Chinese characters during the winter vacation and come to Beijing to discuss the matter in order to realize it as soon as possible.

Ministry of Education Issues Order on Public Officials' Protection Law

The Ministry of Education yesterday issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities and the educational institutions affiliated to the Ministry, stating that, according to the order of the Executive Yuan, before the promulgation and implementation of the Public Officials' Protection Law, all institutions should follow the two orders of March 17 and March 20, and administrative officials should not advance or retreat with political affairs, and qualified personnel who have passed the screening and review should not be dismissed without cause. All relevant departments should comply with this order.

Youth Service Corps Implements Literacy Education During Winter Vacation

Each Member Must Teach at Least Three Illiterate People

(Central News Agency) Nanchang Air Mail: In order to utilize the winter vacation time of the Youth Vacation Service Corps members to implement literacy education, it is stipulated that each member must teach at least three illiterate people, and a list of 100 of the most commonly used characters is attached as teaching materials. The trial implementation measures and the single-character list are recorded as follows:

Measures

Measures for the Trial Implementation of Literacy Education by the Youth Vacation Service Corps During the Winter Vacation. (1) These measures are formulated by this Corps in order to utilize the winter vacation time of the members of this Corps to implement literacy education. (2) Each member should teach at least three illiterate people at home or in the neighborhood so that they can recognize more than 100 commonly used characters (see the attached list of 100 most commonly used single characters). (3) The method of trial implementation of literacy education should be based on the convenience of the person being taught, with door-to-door individual instruction as the principle, and it may also be taught in groups. (4) The trial implementation of literacy education should be based on one hour per day, and each person must have at least ten hours of direct instruction. (5) Before the Corps Headquarters has compiled and issued teaching materials for the trial implementation of literacy education, each member will temporarily adopt their own. It is best to use various mass textbooks or elementary school textbooks as a basis, and string words into sentences according to the single characters listed in the list of 100 most commonly used single characters, and teach them repeatedly. (6) The commonly used characters taught should pay attention to joint application, and the learners should be instructed to practice calligraphy. (7) The trial implementation of literacy education should pay attention to arousing the learners' interest in literacy so that they can continue to study or be admitted to school for instruction (learners in the location of the school will continue to be instructed by the member in their spare time after opening the writing, and learners not in the location of the school should find ways to introduce them to nearby mass schools for instruction in order to achieve complete success). (8) The trial implementation of literacy education should pay attention to persuasion and promote their voluntary instruction, avoiding coercion. (5) The implementation process of the trial implementation of literacy education, and the literacy progress of the learners should have simple records. (10) Corps members with outstanding results in the trial implementation of literacy education will be rewarded at the discretion of the Corps Headquarters after verification.

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM (the 16th), the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education held the opening ceremony of the Provincial School District Social Education Institution Work Discussion Conference in the Department of Education auditorium. High School Outstanding Student Ideological Test Statistics Announced

Majority Hope Chiang Kai-shek Will Serve as President

The Lianyi movement of outstanding students in the second and third grades of high schools, organized by the Municipal Party Headquarters of this city, under the leadership of Tao Baichuan, Yu Zhongbiao, and Wang Longzhang, has been held three times. In addition to the discussion session, the third event included a ten-minute ideological test. A total of 154 people participated in the test. The complete statistics are announced as follows:

(1) Question: What is the meaning of nationalism? 58 people answered completely correctly, 30 people answered two-thirds correctly, 15 people answered one-half correctly, 35 people answered one-third correctly, 2 people did not answer, and 14 people answered completely incorrectly.

(2) Question: What is the meaning of democracy? 51 people answered completely correctly, 36 people answered one-half correctly, 28 people answered one-third correctly, 4 people did not answer, and 35 people answered completely incorrectly.

(3) Question: What is the meaning of people's livelihood? 33 people answered completely correctly, 30 people answered one-half correctly, 53 people answered one-third correctly, 3 people did not answer, and 35 people answered completely incorrectly.

(4) Question: What three works does the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" contain? 50 people answered completely correctly, 45 people answered two-thirds correctly, 12 people answered one-half correctly, 27 people answered one-third correctly, 12 people did not answer, and 8 people answered completely incorrectly.

(5) Question: What do you think is inappropriate about the Three Principles of the People? 109 people answered that there was nothing inappropriate, 14 people answered that there were slight improprieties, 21 people answered that they had no in-depth research and dared not answer rashly, and 10 people did not answer.

(6) Question: What do you think is lacking in the Chinese Nationalist Party compared to other parties? (Or what is not good?) 81 people answered that it was not inferior to other parties, 34 people answered that there were slight deficiencies, 23 people answered that they had no in-depth knowledge and did not dare to answer rashly, and 16 people did not answer.

(7) Question: If China were to elect a president immediately, who would you like to be president and vice president? 93 people answered that they would like to elect Chiang Kai-shek as president, 15 people elected Lin Sen, 5 people elected Wang Jingwei, 4 people elected Hu Hanmin, 1 person elected Soong Ching-ling, 1 person elected Cai Yuanpei, 1 person elected Duan Qirui, 1 person elected Luo Wengan, and 33 people left it blank. 41 people wanted to elect Wang Jingwei as vice president, 26 people elected Chiang Kai-shek, 17 people Lin Sen, 16 people Hu Hanmin, 3 people Sun Ke, 3 people Cai Yuanpei, 1 person Shi Zhaoji, 1 person Yan Huiqing, 1 person Soong Ziwen, 1 person Chen Jitang, 1 person Jiang Kanghu, 1 person Yu Youren, 1 person Wu Tiecheng, and 1 person Ding Wenjiang or Hu Shi, and 40 people left it blank.

(8) Question: Are you willing to join the Chinese Nationalist Party? 80 people answered that they were willing to join, 26 people answered that they were willing to join but could not join at the moment, 24 people answered that they were unwilling to join, 9 people did not answer, 14 people answered that they had already joined, and 1 person was indifferent.

Shanghai Branch of the Educational Film Association Continues to Collect Educational Film Fees

Distributes Letters to Public and Private Schools at All Levels

Collect and Submit Fees for New and Old Students Two Weeks After the Start of the Next Semester

The Shanghai Branch of the China Educational Film Association, which submitted a request to the Ministry of Education for approval last autumn to collect educational film fees from public and private schools at all levels within the city's borders and store them as the association's fund for development, has, since the first semester of the 23rd year, had the Municipal Education Bureau forward the Ministry's order to all schools to comply with the assistance in collection. Students above the vocational school level are charged one yuan each, secondary school students are charged fifty cents each, and elementary school students are charged twenty cents each. This fee is only paid once by each student during their respective academic programs, and will not be collected again. For example, if a first-year student in primary school pays the fee once, they will not have to pay again until they graduate from sixth grade and enter middle school, at which time they will pay the educational film fee for secondary school students once. Many schools at all levels have complied with the order to collect and submit fees to the association this semester. The association has entrusted the collected funds to the Fund Management Committee for special storage. It is now reported that the association needs to collect fees from schools that have not yet collected this semester, and that the educational film fees for new students entering schools next semester should also be collected as required. Therefore, yesterday, letters were sent to schools at all levels, uniformly requiring them to collect and submit the fees within two weeks after the start of the winter vacation, and to submit them to the Municipal Education Bureau for forwarding to all schools for compliance, in order to increase the collection of funds and facilitate the thorough implementation of the plan.

News Roundup from Various Schools

Zhaohe Middle School: Zhaohe Middle School, located at the intersection of Robert Road and Pinlang Road in this city, was originally established with special permission from the Ministry of Education in memory of the Zhaohe warship's uprising. Since its establishment, thanks to the support of the government authorities, the promotion of people from all walks of life, and the cooperation of Principal Jia Botao and all the teachers and students, the school has achieved outstanding results. Furthermore, because the school has always emphasized populism and militarization, the tuition fees are low and the education management is strict. It is reported that there are still a dozen or so vacancies for transfer students in various grades. Entrance examinations will be held at 9:00 AM on January 20 and February 1. Registration will be accepted until the day before the examination date.

Guangzhao Girls' School: Guangzhao Girls' Primary School in North Sichuan Road, Yokohama Bridge, has been in operation for many years and has achieved remarkable results. Currently, there are hundreds of students in various grades. Since Liu Hongwei took over as principal, he has strived to expand the number of students. Therefore, transfer students are being recruited for all grades and kindergartens at the beginning of the spring semester in order to achieve universal education. Registration has begun immediately, and the entrance examination for new students is scheduled for 9:00 AM on the morning of January 26. In recent days, those who have registered to take the exam have been very enthusiastic.

Guoguang Primary School: Guoguang Primary School in Yuyuan Road plans to try out the "little teacher" system during the winter vacation. This system was created by Tao Xingzhi. The school plans to try out this system in the Yuyuan Road area during the holidays. It does not hinder students' studies, and may slightly increase students' interest in self-study during the holidays.

YMCA Day and Night School: Since Cao Yanshen, an Ed.D. from Yale University, took over the YMCA Middle School Day and Night School at the end of last year, internal reforms and student management have been carried out in an orderly manner. The curriculum standards have also been considerably improved. Dr. Cao has been involved in education for fifteen years and has extensive experience and a deep understanding of the psychology of young people. He not only cultivates talent, but also cares about the career prospects of young people after graduation. The school is scheduled to continue recruiting new students in February.

Private Peizhen Primary School: The Private Peizhen Primary School in West Shanghai was initiated and founded by some teachers and staff of the former Nanyang University. The level ranges from kindergarten to the sixth grade of primary school, and the enrollment in each classroom is limited to twenty students. Teaching and management are strictly enforced. After an investigation by the Municipal Education Bureau, the school's performance was rated as excellent and was commended by order. However, due to the limited number of students, most new students are introduced by teachers and students and register in advance, waiting for notification. As a result, it is difficult for children from outside to be admitted. The school authorities have decided to hold two enrollment periods each semester, starting next semester, in order to select students based on merit.
